A large, triangular greenhouse-like building with a steep, sloping roof made primarily of stone bricks and glass panes. The structure has a symmetrical design with the following key features:

A wide base tapering to a point at the top, creating an A-frame silhouette.
Stone brick framework outlining the entire structure, with large glass pane windows filling the spaces between.
A central column of oak planks running from the base to the peak, bisecting the front facade.
Two wing-like protrusions on either side of the main structure, also made of stone bricks and glass.
A small, wooden door at the base of the central oak plank column.
The foundation is made of cobblestone, transitioning into the stone brick frame.
Abundant vegetation growing inside and around the structure, visible through the glass panes.
A complex, patterned path leading up to the entrance, made of various materials including stone, wood planks, and grass blocks.
Surrounding landscape features including trees, flowers, and custom-made details like small fences and posts.
